 *                   10000         :  Preconditioning calls
 *                      10         :  Preconditioning iterations
 *                  1.0000         :  Percentage accuracy
 *                   10000         :  Calls in first main iteration
 *                   10000         :  Increase calls per iteration
 *                    1000         :  Maximum number of iterations
 *                     177         :  Random number seed
 **********************************************************                                                            **************
 *                       8         : Survival factor integration par.
 **********************************************************                                                            **************
 
 ********************* Unweighted Events  *****************                                                            **************
 *                       T         :  Generate unweighted events
 *                   50000         :  Number of events
 *                     lhe         : Record format
 **********************************************************                                                            **************
 
 ********************* General Cuts ***********************                                                            **************
 *                -10.0000         :  Minimum object rapidity
 *                 10.0000         :  Maximum object rapidity
 *                  2.0000         :  Minimum object mass
 *               5000.0000         :  Maximum object mass
 *                       T         :  Include further cuts
 *                       T         :  Include spin correlations
 **********************************************************                                                            **************
 
 ***************** 2-body decay cuts **********************                                                            **************
 *                  0.0000         :  pT(a) min
